ASSERT(connecting_stream_capacity_ == 0);\n    34→}\n    35→\n    36→void ConnPoolImplBase::deleteIsPendingImpl() {\n    37→  deferred_deleting_ = true;\n    38→  ASSERT(isIdleImpl());\n    39→  ASSERT(connecting_stream_capacity_ == 0);\n    40→}\n    41→\n    42→void ConnPoolImplBase::destructAllConnections() {\n    43→  for (auto* list : {&ready_clients_, &busy_clients_, &connecting_clients_, &early_data_clients_}) {\n    44→    while (!list->empty()) {\n    45→      list->front()->close();\n    46→    }\n    47→  }\n    48→\n    49→  // Make sure all clients are destroyed before we are destroyed.\n    50→  dispatcher_.clearDeferredDeleteList();\n    51→}\n    52→\n    53→bool ConnPoolImplBase::shouldConnect(size_t pending_streams, size_t active_streams,\n    54→                                     int64_t connecting_and_connected_capacity,\n    55→                                     float preconnect_ratio, bool anticipate_incoming_stream) {\n    56→  // This is set to true any time global preconnect is being calculated.\n    57→  // ClusterManagerImpl::maybePreconnect is called directly before a stream is created, so the\n    58→  // stream must be anticipated.\n    59→  //\n    60→  // Also without this, we would never pre-establish a connection as the first\n    61→  // connection in a pool because pending/active streams could both be 0.\n    62→  int anticipated_streams = anticipate_incoming_stream ? 1 : 0;\n    63→\n    64→  // The number of streams we want to be provisioned for is the number of\n    65→  // pending, active, and anticipated streams times the preconnect ratio.\n    66→  // The number of streams we are (theoretically) provisioned for is the\n    67→  // connecting stream capacity plus the number of active streams.\n    68→  //\n    69→  // If preconnect ratio is not set, it defaults to 1, and this simplifies to the\n    70→  // legacy value of pending_streams_.size() > connecting_stream_capacity_\n    71→  return (pending_streams + active_streams + anticipated_streams) * preconnect_ratio >\n    72→         connecting_and_connected_capacity + active_streams;\n    73→}\n    74→\n    75→bool ConnPoolImplBase::shouldCreateNewConnection(float global_preconnect_ratio) const {\n    76→  // If the host is not healthy, don't make it do extra work, especially as\n    77→  // upstream selection logic may result in bypassing this upstream entirely.\n    78→  // If an Envoy user wants preconnecting for degraded upstreams this could be\n    79→  // added later via extending the preconnect config.\n    80→  if (host_->coarseHealth() != Upstream::Host::Health::Healthy) {\n    81→    return pending_streams_.size() > connecting_stream_capacity_;\n    82→  }\n    83→\n    84→  // Determine if we are trying to prefetch for global preconnect or local preconnect.\n    85→  if (global_preconnect_ratio != 0) {\n    86→    // If global preconnecting is on, and this connection is within the global\n    87→    // preconnect limit, preconnect.\n    88→    // For global preconnect, we anticipate an incoming stream to this pool, since it is\n    89→    // prefetching for the next upcoming stream, which will likely be assigned to this pool.\n    90→    // We may eventually want to track preconnect_attempts to allow more preconnecting for\n    91→    // heavily weighted upstreams or sticky picks.\n    92→    return shouldConnect(pending_streams_.size(), num_active_streams_, connecting_stream_capacity_,\n    93→                         global_preconnect_ratio, true);\n    94→  } else {\n    95→    // Ensure this local pool has adequate connections for the given load.\n    96→    //\n    97→    // Local preconnect does not need to anticipate a stream. It is called as\n    98→    // new streams are established or torn down and simply attempts to maintain\n    99→    // the correct ratio of streams and anticipated capacity.\n   100→    return shouldConnect(pending_streams_.size(), num_active_streams_, connecting_stream_capacity_,\n   101→                         perUpstreamPreconnectRatio());\n   102→  }\n   103→}\n   104→\n   105→float ConnPoolImplBase::perUpstreamPreconnectRatio() const {\n   106→  return host_->cluster().perUpstreamPreconnectRatio();\n   107→}\n   108→\n   109→ConnPoolImplBase::ConnectionResult ConnPoolImplBase::tryCreateNewConnections() {\n   110→  ConnPoolImplBase::ConnectionResult result;\n   111→  // Somewhat arbitrarily cap the number of connections preconnected due to new\n   112→  // incoming connections. The preconnect ratio is capped at 3, so in steady\n   113→  // state, no more than 3 connections should be preconnected. If hosts go\n   114→  // unhealthy, and connections are not immediately preconnected, it could be that\n   115→  // many connections are desired when the host becomes healthy again, but\n   116→  // overwhelming it with connections is not desirable.\n   117→  for (int i = 0; i < 3; ++i) {\n   118→    result = tryCreateNewConnection();\n   119→    if (result != ConnectionResult::CreatedNewConnection) {\n   120→      break;\n   121→    }\n   122→  }\n   123→  ASSERT(!is_draining_for_deletion_ || result != ConnectionResult::CreatedNewConnection);\n   124→  return result;\n   125→}\n   126→\n   127→ConnPoolImplBase::ConnectionResult\n   128→ConnPoolImplBase::tryCreateNewConnection(float global_preconnect_ratio) {\n   129→  // There are already enough Connecting connections for the number of queued streams.\n   130→  if (!shouldCreateNewConnection(global_preconnect_ratio)) {\n   131→    ENVOY_LOG(trace, \"not creating a new connection, shouldCreateNewConnection returned false.\");\n   132→    return ConnectionResult::ShouldNotConnect;\n   133→  }\n   134→\n   135→  const bool can_create_connection = host_->canCreateConnection(priority_);\n   136→\n   137→  if (!can_create_connection) {\n   138→    host_->cluster().trafficStats()->upstream_cx_overflow_.inc();\n   139→  }\n   140→  // If we are at the connection circuit-breaker limit due to other upstreams having\n   141→  // too many open connections, and this upstream has no connections, always create one, to\n   142→  // prevent pending streams being queued to this upstream with no way to be processed.\n   143→  if (can_create_connection || (ready_clients_.empty() && busy_clients_.empty() &&\n   144→                                connecting_clients_.empty() && early_data_clients_.empty())) {\n   145→    ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"creating a new connection (connecting={})\", connecting_clients_.size());\n   146→    ActiveClientPtr client = instantiateActiveClient();\n   147→    if (client.get() == nullptr) {\n   148→      ENVOY_LOG(trace, \"connection creation failed\");\n   149→      return ConnectionResult::FailedToCreateConnection;\n   150→    }\n   151→    ASSERT(client->state() == ActiveClient::State::Connecting);\n   152→    ASSERT(std::numeric_limits<uint64_t>::max() - connecting_stream_capacity_ >=\n   153→           static_cast<uint64_t>(client->currentUnusedCapacity()));\n   154→    ASSERT(client->real_host_description_);\n   155→    // Increase the connecting capacity to reflect the streams this connection can serve.\n   156→    incrConnectingAndConnectedStreamCapacity(client->currentUnusedCapacity(), *client);\n   157→    LinkedList::moveIntoList(std::move(client), owningList(client->state()));\n   158→    return can_create_connection ? ConnectionResult::CreatedNewConnection\n   159→                                 : ConnectionResult::CreatedButRateLimited;\n   160→  } else {\n   161→    ENVOY_LOG(trace, \"not creating a new connection: connection constrained\");\n   162→    return ConnectionResult::NoConnectionRateLimited;\n   163→  }\n   164→}\n   165→\n   166→void ConnPoolImplBase::attachStreamToClient(Envoy::ConnectionPool::ActiveClient& client,\n   167→                                            AttachContext& context) {\n   168→  ASSERT(client.readyForStream());\n   169→\n   170→  Upstream::ClusterTrafficStats& traffic_stats = *host_->cluster().trafficStats();\n   171→  if (client.state() == Envoy::ConnectionPool::ActiveClient::State::ReadyForEarlyData) {\n   172→    traffic_stats.upstream_rq_0rtt_.inc();\n   173→  }\n   174→\n   175→  if (enforceMaxRequests() && !host_->cluster().resourceManager(priority_).requests().canCreate()) {\n   176→    ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"max streams overflow\");\n   177→    onPoolFailure(client.real_host_description_, absl::string_view(),\n   178→                  ConnectionPool::PoolFailureReason::Overflow, context);\n   179→    traffic_stats.upstream_rq_pending_overflow_.inc();\n   180→    return;\n   181→  }\n   182→  ENVOY_CONN_LOG(debug, \"creating stream\", client);\n   183→\n   184→  // Latch capacity before updating remaining streams.\n   185→  uint64_t capacity = client.currentUnusedCapacity();\n   186→  client.remaining_streams_--;\n   187→  if (client.remaining_streams_ == 0) {\n   188→    ENVOY_CONN_LOG(debug, \"maximum streams per connection, start draining\", client);\n   189→    traffic_stats.upstream_cx_max_requests_.inc();\n   190→    transitionActiveClientState(client, Envoy::ConnectionPool::ActiveClient::State::Draining);\n   191→  } else if (capacity == 1) {\n   192→    // As soon as the new stream is created, the client will be maxed out.\n   193→    transitionActiveClientState(client, Envoy::ConnectionPool::ActiveClient::State::Busy);\n   194→  }\n   195→\n   196→  // Decrement the capacity, as there's one less stream available for serving.\n   197→  // For HTTP/3, the capacity is updated in newStreamEncoder.\n   198→  if (trackStreamCapacity()) {\n   199→    decrConnectingAndConnectedStreamCapacity(1, client);\n   200→  }\n   201→  // Track the new active stream.\n   202→  state_.incrActiveStreams(1);\n   203→  num_active_streams_++;\n   204→  host_->stats().rq_total_.inc();\n   205→  host_->stats().rq_active_.inc();\n   206→  traffic_stats.upstream_rq_total_.inc();\n   207→  traffic_stats.upstream_rq_active_.inc();\n   208→  host_->cluster().resourceManager(priority_).requests().inc();\n   209→\n   210→  onPoolReady(client, context);\n   211→}\n   212→\n   213→void ConnPoolImplBase::onStreamClosed(Envoy::ConnectionPool::ActiveClient& client,\n   214→                                      bool delay_attaching_stream) {\n   215→  ENVOY_CONN_LOG(debug, \"destroying stream: {} remaining\", client, client.numActiveStreams());\n   216→  ASSERT(num_active_streams_ > 0);\n   217→  state_.decrActiveStreams(1);\n   218→  num_active_streams_--;\n   219→  host_->stats().rq_active_.dec();\n   220→  host_->cluster().trafficStats()->upstream_rq_active_.dec();\n   221→  host_->cluster().resourceManager(priority_).requests().dec();\n   222→  // We don't update the capacity for HTTP/3 as the stream count should only\n   223→  // increase when a MAX_STREAMS frame is received.\n   224→  if (trackStreamCapacity()) {\n   225→    // If the effective client capacity was limited by concurrency, increase connecting capacity.\n   226→    bool limited_by_concurrency =\n   227→        client.remaining_streams_ > client.concurrent_stream_limit_ - client.numActiveStreams() - 1;\n   228→    // The capacity calculated by concurrency could be negative if a SETTINGS frame lowered the\n   229→    // number of allowed streams. In this case, effective client capacity was still limited by\n   230→    // concurrency, compare client.concurrent_stream_limit_ and client.numActiveStreams() directly\n   231→    // to avoid overflow.\n   232→    bool negative_capacity = client.concurrent_stream_limit_ < client.numActiveStreams() + 1;\n   233→    if (negative_capacity || limited_by_concurrency) {\n   234→      incrConnectingAndConnectedStreamCapacity(1, client);\n   235→    }\n   236→  }\n   237→  if (client.state() == ActiveClient::State::Draining && client.numActiveStreams() == 0) {\n   238→    // Close out the draining client if we no longer have active streams.\n   239→    client.close();\n   240→  } else if (client.state() == ActiveClient::State::Busy && client.currentUnusedCapacity() > 0) {\n   241→    if (!client.hasHandshakeCompleted()) {\n   242→      transitionActiveClientState(client, ActiveClient::State::ReadyForEarlyData);\n   243→      if (!delay_attaching_stream) {\n   244→        onUpstreamReadyForEarlyData(client);\n   245→      }\n   246→    } else {\n   247→      transitionActiveClientState(client, ActiveClient::State::Ready);\n   248→      if (!delay_attaching_stream) {\n   249→        onUpstreamReady();\n   250→      }\n   251→    }\n   252→  }\n   253→}\n   254→\n   255→ConnectionPool::Cancellable* ConnPoolImplBase::newStreamImpl(AttachContext& context,\n   256→                                                             bool can_send_early_data) {\n   257→  ASSERT(!is_draining_for_deletion_);\n   258→  ASSERT(!deferred_deleting_);\n   259→\n   260→  ASSERT(static_cast<ssize_t>(connecting_stream_capacity_) ==\n   261→         connectingCapacity(connecting_clients_) +\n   262→             connectingCapacity(early_data_clients_)); // O(n) debug check.\n   263→  if (!ready_clients_.empty()) {\n   264→    ActiveClient& client = *ready_clients_.front();\n   265→    ENVOY_CONN_LOG(debug, \"using existing fully connected connection\", client);\n   266→    attachStreamToClient(client, context);\n   267→    // Even if there's a ready client, we may want to preconnect to handle the next incoming stream.\n   268→    tryCreateNewConnections();\n   269→    return nullptr;\n   270→  }\n   271→\n   272→  if (can_send_early_data && !early_data_clients_.empty()) {\n   273→    ActiveClient& client = *early_data_clients_.front();\n   274→    ENVOY_CONN_LOG(debug, \"using existing early data ready connection\", client);\n   275→    attachStreamToClient(client, context);\n   276→    // Even if there's an available client, we may want to preconnect to handle the next\n   277→    // incoming stream.\n   278→    tryCreateNewConnections();\n   279→    return nullptr;\n   280→  }\n   281→\n   282→  if (!host_->cluster().resourceManager(priority_).pendingRequests().canCreate()) {\n   283→    ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"max pending streams overflow\");\n   284→    onPoolFailure(nullptr, absl::string_view(), ConnectionPool::PoolFailureReason::Overflow,\n   285→                  context);\n   286→    host_->cluster().trafficStats()->upstream_rq_pending_overflow_.inc();\n   287→    return nullptr;\n   288→  }\n   289→\n   290→  ConnectionPool::Cancellable* pending = newPendingStream(context, can_send_early_data);\n   291→  ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"trying to create new connection\");\n   292→  ENVOY_LOG(trace, fmt::format(\"{}\", *this));\n   293→\n   294→  auto old_capacity = connecting_stream_capacity_;\n   295→  // This must come after newPendingStream() because this function uses the\n   296→  // length of pending_streams_ to determine if a new connection is needed.\n   297→  const ConnectionResult result = tryCreateNewConnections();\n   298→  // If there is not enough connecting capacity, the only reason to not\n   299→  // increase capacity is if the connection limits are exceeded.\n   300→  ENVOY_BUG(pending_streams_.size() <= connecting_stream_capacity_ ||\n   301→                connecting_stream_capacity_ > old_capacity ||\n   302→                (result == ConnectionResult::NoConnectionRateLimited ||\n   303→                 result == ConnectionResult::FailedToCreateConnection),\n   304→            fmt::format(\"Failed to create expected connection: {}\", *this));\n   305→  if (result == ConnectionResult::FailedToCreateConnection) {\n   306→    // This currently only happens for HTTP/3 if secrets aren't yet loaded.\n   307→    // Trigger connection failure.\n   308→    pending->cancel(Envoy::ConnectionPool::CancelPolicy::CloseExcess);\n   309→    onPoolFailure(nullptr, absl::string_view(),\n   310→                  ConnectionPool::PoolFailureReason::LocalConnectionFailure, context);\n   311→    return nullptr;\n   312→  }\n   313→  return pending;\n   314→}\n   315→\n   316→bool ConnPoolImplBase::maybePreconnectImpl(float global_preconnect_ratio) {\n   317→  ASSERT(!deferred_deleting_);\n   318→  return tryCreateNewConnection(global_preconnect_ratio) == ConnectionResult::CreatedNewConnection;\n   319→}\n   320→\n   321→void ConnPoolImplBase::scheduleOnUpstreamReady() {\n   322→  upstream_ready_cb_->scheduleCallbackCurrentIteration();\n   323→}\n   324→\n   325→void ConnPoolImplBase::onUpstreamReady() {\n   326→  while (!pending_streams_.empty() && !ready_clients_.empty()) {\n   327→    ActiveClientPtr& client = ready_clients_.front();\n   328→    ENVOY_CONN_LOG(debug, \"attaching to next stream\", *client);\n   329→    // Pending streams are pushed onto the front, so pull from the back.\n   330→    attachStreamToClient(*client, pending_streams_.back()->context());\n   331→    state_.decrPendingStreams(1);\n   332→    pending_streams_.pop_back();\n   333→  }\n   334→  if (!pending_streams_.empty()) {\n   335→    tryCreateNewConnections();\n   336→  }\n   337→}\n   338→\n   339→std::list<ActiveClientPtr>& ConnPoolImplBase::owningList(ActiveClient::State state) {\n   340→  switch (state) {\n   341→  case ActiveClient::State::Connecting:\n   342→    return connecting_clients_;\n   343→  case ActiveClient::State::ReadyForEarlyData:\n   344→    return early_data_clients_;\n   345→  case ActiveClient::State::Ready:\n   346→    return ready_clients_;\n   347→  case ActiveClient::State::Busy:\n   348→  case ActiveClient::State::Draining:\n   349→    return busy_clients_;\n   350→  case ActiveClient::State::Closed:\n   351→    break; // Fall through to PANIC.\n   352→  }\n   353→  PANIC(\"unexpected\");\n   354→}\n   355→\n   356→void ConnPoolImplBase::transitionActiveClientState(ActiveClient& client,\n   357→                                                   ActiveClient::State new_state) {\n   358→  auto& old_list = owningList(client.state());\n   359→  auto& new_list = owningList(new_state);\n   360→  client.setState(new_state);\n   361→\n   362→  // old_list and new_list can be equal when transitioning from Busy to Draining.\n   363→  //\n   364→  // The documentation for list.splice() (which is what moveBetweenLists() calls) is\n   365→  // unclear whether it is allowed for src and dst to be the same, so check here\n   366→  // since it is a no-op anyways.\n   367→  if (&old_list != &new_list) {\n   368→    client.moveBetweenLists(old_list, new_list);\n   369→  }\n   370→}\n   371→\n   372→void ConnPoolImplBase::addIdleCallbackImpl(Instance::IdleCb cb) { idle_callbacks_.push_back(cb); }\n   373→\n   374→void ConnPoolImplBase::closeIdleConnectionsForDrainingPool() {\n   375→  Common::AutoDebugRecursionChecker assert_not_in(recursion_checker_);\n   376→\n   377→  // Create a separate list of elements to close to avoid mutate-while-iterating problems.\n   378→  std::list<ActiveClient*> to_close;\n   379→\n   380→  for (auto& client : ready_clients_) {\n   381→    if (client->numActiveStreams() == 0) {\n   382→      to_close.push_back(client.get());\n   383→    }\n   384→  }\n   385→\n   386→  if (pending_streams_.empty()) {\n   387→    for (auto& client : connecting_clients_) {\n   388→      to_close.push_back(client.get());\n   389→    }\n   390→    for (auto& client : early_data_clients_) {\n   391→      if (client->numActiveStreams() == 0) {\n   392→        to_close.push_back(client.get());\n   393→      }\n   394→    }\n   395→  }\n   396→\n   397→  for (auto& entry : to_close) {\n   398→    ENVOY_LOG_EVENT(debug, \"closing_idle_client\", \"closing idle client {} for cluster {}\",\n   399→                    entry->id(), host_->cluster().name());\n   400→    entry->close();\n   401→  }\n   402→}\n   403→\n   404→void ConnPoolImplBase::drainClients(std::list<ActiveClientPtr>& clients) {\n   405→  while (!clients.empty()) {\n   406→    ASSERT(clients.front()->numActiveStreams() > 0u);\n   407→    ENVOY_LOG_EVENT(\n   408→        debug, \"draining_non_idle_client\", \"draining {} client {} for cluster {}\",\n   409→        (clients.front()->state() == ActiveClient::State::Ready ? \"ready\" : \"early data\"),\n   410→        clients.front()->id(), host_->cluster().name());\n   411→    transitionActiveClientState(*clients.front(), ActiveClient::State::Draining);\n   412→  }\n   413→}\n   414→\n   415→void ConnPoolImplBase::drainConnectionsImpl(DrainBehavior drain_behavior) {\n   416→  if (drain_behavior == Envoy::ConnectionPool::DrainBehavior::DrainAndDelete) {\n   417→    is_draining_for_deletion_ = true;\n   418→    checkForIdleAndCloseIdleConnsIfDraining();\n   419→    return;\n   420→  }\n   421→  closeIdleConnectionsForDrainingPool();\n   422→  // closeIdleConnectionsForDrainingPool() closes all connections in ready_clients_ with no active\n   423→  // streams and if no pending streams, all connections in early_data_clients_ with no active\n   424→  // streams as well, so all remaining entries in ready_clients_ are serving streams. Move them and\n   425→  // all entries in busy_clients_ to draining.\n   426→  if (pending_streams_.empty()) {\n   427→    // The remaining early data clients are non-idle.\n   428→    drainClients(early_data_clients_);\n   429→  }\n   430→\n   431→  drainClients(ready_clients_);\n   432→\n   433→  // Changing busy_clients_ to Draining does not move them between lists,\n   434→  // so use a for-loop since the list is not mutated.\n   435→  ASSERT(&owningList(ActiveClient::State::Draining) == &busy_clients_);\n   436→  for (auto& busy_client : busy_clients_) {\n   437→    if (busy_client->state() == ActiveClient::State::Draining) {\n   438→      continue;\n   439→    }\n   440→    ENVOY_LOG_EVENT(debug, \"draining_busy_client\", \"draining busy client {} for cluster {}\",\n   441→                    busy_client->id(), host_->cluster().name());\n   442→    transitionActiveClientState(*busy_client, ActiveClient::State::Draining);\n   443→  }\n   444→}\n   445→\n   446→bool ConnPoolImplBase::isIdleImpl() const {\n   447→  return pending_streams_.empty() && ready_clients_.empty() && busy_clients_.empty() &&\n   448→         connecting_clients_.empty() && early_data_clients_.empty();\n   449→}\n   450→\n   451→/*\n   452→  This method may be invoked once or twice.\n   453→  It is called first time in ConnPoolImplBase::onConnectionEvent for Local/RemoteClose events.\n   454→  The second time it is called from Envoy::Tcp::ActiveTcpClient::~ActiveTcpClient via\n   455→  ConnPoolImplBase::checkForIdleAndCloseIdleConnsIfDraining.\n   456→\n   457→  The logic must be constructed in such way that the method is called once or twice.\n   458→  See PR 30807 description for explanation why idle callbacks are deleted after being called.\n   459→*/\n   460→void ConnPoolImplBase::checkForIdleAndNotify() {\n   461→  if (isIdleImpl()) {\n   462→    ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"invoking {} idle callback(s) - is_draining_for_deletion_={}\",\n   463→              idle_callbacks_.size(), is_draining_for_deletion_);\n   464→    for (const Instance::IdleCb& cb : idle_callbacks_) {\n   465→      cb();\n   466→    }\n   467→    // Clear callbacks, so they are not executed if checkForIdleAndNotify is called again.\n   468→    idle_callbacks_.clear();\n   469→  }\n   470→}\n   471→\n   472→void ConnPoolImplBase::checkForIdleAndCloseIdleConnsIfDraining() {\n   473→  if (is_draining_for_deletion_) {\n   474→    closeIdleConnectionsForDrainingPool();\n   475→  }\n   476→\n   477→  checkForIdleAndNotify();\n   478→}\n   479→\n   480→void ConnPoolImplBase::onConnectionEvent(ActiveClient& client, absl::string_view failure_reason,\n   481→                                         Network::ConnectionEvent event) {\n   482→  switch (event) {\n   483→  case Network::ConnectionEvent::RemoteClose:\n   484→  case Network::ConnectionEvent::LocalClose: {\n   485→    if (client.connect_timer_) {\n   486→      ASSERT(!client.has_handshake_completed_);\n   487→      client.connect_timer_->disableTimer();\n   488→      client.connect_timer_.reset();\n   489→    }\n   490→    decrConnectingAndConnectedStreamCapacity(client.currentUnusedCapacity(), client);\n   491→\n   492→    // Make sure that onStreamClosed won't double count.\n   493→    client.remaining_streams_ = 0;\n   494→    // The client died.\n   495→    ENVOY_CONN_LOG(debug, \"client disconnected, failure reason: {}\", client, failure_reason);\n   496→\n   497→    Envoy::Upstream::reportUpstreamCxDestroy(host_, event);\n   498→    const bool incomplete_stream = client.closingWithIncompleteStream();\n   499→    if (incomplete_stream) {\n   500→      Envoy::Upstream::reportUpstreamCxDestroyActiveRequest(host_, event);\n   501→    }\n   502→\n   503→    if (!client.hasHandshakeCompleted()) {\n   504→      client.has_handshake_completed_ = true;\n   505→      host_->cluster().trafficStats()->upstream_cx_connect_fail_.inc();\n   506→      host_->stats().cx_connect_fail_.inc();\n   507→\n   508→      onConnectFailed(client);\n   509→      // Purge pending streams only if this client doesn't contribute to the local connecting\n   510→      // stream capacity. In other words, the rest clients  would be able to handle all the\n   511→      // pending stream once they are connected.\n   512→      ConnectionPool::PoolFailureReason reason;\n   513→      if (client.timed_out_) {\n   514→        reason = ConnectionPool::PoolFailureReason::Timeout;\n   515→      } else if (event == Network::ConnectionEvent::RemoteClose) {\n   516→        reason = ConnectionPool::PoolFailureReason::RemoteConnectionFailure;\n   517→      } else {\n   518→        reason = ConnectionPool::PoolFailureReason::LocalConnectionFailure;\n   519→      }\n   520→\n   521→      // Raw connect failures should never happen under normal circumstances. If we have an\n   522→      // upstream that is behaving badly, streams can get stuck here in the pending state. If we\n   523→      // see a connect failure, we purge all pending streams so that calling code can determine\n   524→      // what to do with the stream.\n   525→      // NOTE: We move the existing pending streams to a temporary list. This is done so that\n   526→      //       if retry logic submits a new stream to the pool, we don't fail it inline.\n   527→      purgePendingStreams(client.real_host_description_, failure_reason, reason);\n   528→      // See if we should preconnect based on active connections.\n   529→      if (!is_draining_for_deletion_) {\n   530→        tryCreateNewConnections();\n   531→      }\n   532→    }\n   533→\n   534→    // We need to release our resourceManager() resources before checking below for\n   535→    // whether we can create a new connection. Normally this would happen when\n   536→    // client's destructor runs, but this object needs to be deferredDelete'd(), so\n   537→    // this forces part of its cleanup to happen now.\n   538→    client.releaseResources();\n   539→\n   540→    // Again, since we know this object is going to be deferredDelete'd(), we take\n   541→    // this opportunity to disable and reset the connection duration timer so that\n   542→    // it doesn't trigger while on the deferred delete list. In theory it is safe\n   543→    // to handle the Closed state in onConnectionDurationTimeout, but we handle\n   544→    // it here for simplicity and safety anyway.\n   545→    if (client.connection_duration_timer_) {\n   546→      client.connection_duration_timer_->disableTimer();\n   547→      client.connection_duration_timer_.reset();\n   548→    }\n   549→\n   550→    dispatcher_.deferredDelete(client.removeFromList(owningList(client.state())));\n   551→\n   552→    // Check if the pool transitioned to idle state after removing closed client\n   553→    // from one of the client tracking lists.\n   554→    // There is no need to check if other connections are idle in a draining pool\n   555→    // because the pool will close all idle connection when it is starting to\n   556→    // drain.\n   557→    // Trying to close other connections here can lead to deep recursion when\n   558→    // a large number idle connections are closed at the start of pool drain.\n   559→    // See CdsIntegrationTest.CdsClusterDownWithLotsOfIdleConnections for an example.\n   560→    checkForIdleAndNotify();\n   561→\n   562→    client.setState(ActiveClient::State::Closed);\n   563→\n   564→    // If we have pending streams and we just lost a connection we should make a new one.\n   565→    if (!pending_streams_.empty()) {\n   566→      tryCreateNewConnections();\n   567→    }\n   568→    break;\n   569→  }\n   570→  case Network::ConnectionEvent::Connected: {\n   571→    ASSERT(client.connect_timer_ != nullptr && !client.has_handshake_completed_);\n   572→    client.connect_timer_->disableTimer();\n   573→    client.connect_timer_.reset();\n   574→\n   575→    ASSERT(connecting_stream_capacity_ >= client.currentUnusedCapacity());\n   576→    connecting_stream_capacity_ -= client.currentUnusedCapacity();\n   577→    client.has_handshake_completed_ = true;\n   578→    client.conn_connect_ms_->complete();\n   579→    client.conn_connect_ms_.reset();\n   580→    if (client.state() == ActiveClient::State::Connecting ||\n   581→        client.state() == ActiveClient::State::ReadyForEarlyData) {\n   582→      transitionActiveClientState(client,\n   583→                                  (client.currentUnusedCapacity() > 0 ? ActiveClient::State::Ready\n   584→                                                                      : ActiveClient::State::Busy));\n   585→    }\n   586→\n   587→    // Now that the active client is ready, set up a timer for max connection duration.\n   588→    const absl::optional<std::chrono::milliseconds> max_connection_duration =\n   589→        client.parent_.host()->cluster().maxConnectionDuration();\n   590→    if (max_connection_duration.has_value()) {\n   591→      client.connection_duration_timer_ = client.parent_.dispatcher().createTimer(\n   592→          [&client]() { client.onConnectionDurationTimeout(); });\n   593→      client.connection_duration_timer_->enableTimer(max_connection_duration.value());\n   594→    }\n   595→    // Initialize client read filters\n   596→    client.initializeReadFilters();\n   597→\n   598→    // At this point, for the mixed ALPN pool, the client may be deleted. Do not\n   599→    // refer to client after this point.\n   600→    onConnected(client);\n   601→    if (client.readyForStream()) {\n   602→      onUpstreamReady();\n   603→    }\n   604→    checkForIdleAndCloseIdleConnsIfDraining();\n   605→    break;\n   606→  }\n   607→  case Network::ConnectionEvent::ConnectedZeroRtt: {\n   608→    ENVOY_CONN_LOG(debug, \"0-RTT connected with capacity {}\", client,\n   609→                   client.currentUnusedCapacity());\n   610→    // No need to update connecting capacity and connect_timer_ as the client is still connecting.\n   611→    ASSERT(client.state() == ActiveClient::State::Connecting);\n   612→    host()->cluster().trafficStats()->upstream_cx_connect_with_0_rtt_.inc();\n   613→    transitionActiveClientState(client, (client.currentUnusedCapacity() > 0\n   614→                                             ? ActiveClient::State::ReadyForEarlyData\n   615→                                             : ActiveClient::State::Busy));\n   616→    break;\n   617→  }\n   618→  }\n   619→}\n   620→\n   621→PendingStream::PendingStream(ConnPoolImplBase& parent, bool can_send_early_data)\n   622→    : parent_(parent), can_send_early_data_(can_send_early_data) {\n   623→  Upstream::ClusterTrafficStats& traffic_stats = *parent_.host()->cluster().trafficStats();\n   624→  traffic_stats.upstream_rq_pending_total_.inc();\n   625→  traffic_stats.upstream_rq_pending_active_.inc();\n   626→  parent_.host()->cluster().resourceManager(parent_.priority()).pendingRequests().inc();\n   627→}\n   628→\n   629→PendingStream::~PendingStream() {\n   630→  parent_.host()->cluster().trafficStats()->upstream_rq_pending_active_.dec();\n   631→  parent_.host()->cluster().resourceManager(parent_.priority()).pendingRequests().dec();\n   632→}\n   633→\n   634→void PendingStream::cancel(Envoy::ConnectionPool::CancelPolicy policy) {\n   635→  parent_.onPendingStreamCancel(*this, policy);\n   636→}\n   637→\n   638→void ConnPoolImplBase::purgePendingStreams(\n   639→    const Upstream::HostDescriptionConstSharedPtr& host_description,\n   640→    absl::string_view failure_reason, ConnectionPool::PoolFailureReason reason) {\n   641→  // NOTE: We move the existing pending streams to a temporary list. This is done so that\n   642→  //       if retry logic submits a new stream to the pool, we don't fail it inline.\n   643→  state_.decrPendingStreams(pending_streams_.size());\n   644→  pending_streams_to_purge_ = std::move(pending_streams_);\n   645→  while (!pending_streams_to_purge_.empty()) {\n   646→    PendingStreamPtr stream =\n   647→        pending_streams_to_purge_.front()->removeFromList(pending_streams_to_purge_);\n   648→    host_->cluster().trafficStats()->upstream_rq_pending_failure_eject_.inc();\n   649→    onPoolFailure(host_description, failure_reason, reason, stream->context());\n   650→  }\n   651→}\n   652→\n   653→bool ConnPoolImplBase::connectingConnectionIsExcess(const ActiveClient& client) const {\n   654→  ASSERT(!client.hasHandshakeCompleted());\n   655→  ASSERT(connecting_stream_capacity_ >= client.currentUnusedCapacity());\n   656→  // If perUpstreamPreconnectRatio is one, this simplifies to checking if there would still be\n   657→  // sufficient connecting stream capacity to serve all pending streams if the most recent client\n   658→  // were removed from the picture.\n   659→  //\n   660→  // If preconnect ratio is set, it also factors in the anticipated load based on both queued\n   661→  // streams and active streams, and makes sure the connecting capacity would still be sufficient to\n   662→  // serve that even with the most recent client removed.\n   663→  return (pending_streams_.size() + num_active_streams_) * perUpstreamPreconnectRatio() <=\n   664→         (connecting_stream_capacity_ - client.currentUnusedCapacity() + num_active_streams_);\n   665→}\n   666→\n   667→void ConnPoolImplBase::onPendingStreamCancel(PendingStream& stream,\n   668→                                             Envoy::ConnectionPool::CancelPolicy policy) {\n   669→  ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"cancelling pending stream\");\n   670→  if (!pending_streams_to_purge_.empty()) {\n   671→    // If pending_streams_to_purge_ is not empty, it means that we are called from\n   672→    // with-in a onPoolFailure callback invoked in purgePendingStreams (i.e. purgePendingStreams\n   673→    // is down in the call stack). ConnPoolImplBase::destructAllConnections() {\n  for (auto* list : {&ready_clients_, &busy_clients_, &connecting_clients_, &early_data_clients_}) {\n    while (!list->empty()) {\n      list->front()->close();\n    }\n  }\n\n  // Make sure all clients are destroyed before we are destroyed.\n  dispatcher_.clearDeferredDeleteList();\n}\n\nbool ConnPoolImplBase::shouldConnect(size_t pending_streams, size_t active_streams,\n                                     int64_t connecting_and_connected_capacity,\n                                     float preconnect_ratio, bool anticipate_incoming_stream) {\n  // This is set to true any time global preconnect is being calculated.\n  // ClusterManagerImpl::maybePreconnect is called directly before a stream is created, so the\n  // stream must be anticipated.\n  //\n  // Also without this, we would never pre-establish a connection as the first\n  // connection in a pool because pending/active streams could both be 0.\n  int anticipated_streams = anticipate_incoming_stream ? 1 : 0;\n\n  // The number of streams we want to be provisioned for is the number of\n  // pending, active, and anticipated streams times the preconnect ratio.\n  // The number of streams we are (theoretically) provisioned for is the\n  // connecting stream capacity plus the number of active streams.\n  //\n  // If preconnect ratio is not set, it defaults to 1, and this simplifies to the\n  // legacy value of pending_streams_.size() > connecting_stream_capacity_\n  return (pending_streams + active_streams + anticipated_streams) * preconnect_ratio >\n         connecting_and_connected_capacity + active_streams;\n}\n\nbool ConnPoolImplBase::shouldCreateNewConnection(float global_preconnect_ratio) const {\n  // If the host is not healthy, don't make it do extra work, especially as\n  // upstream selection logic may result in bypassing this upstream entirely.\n  // If an Envoy user wants preconnecting for degraded upstreams this could be\n  // added later via extending the preconnect config.\n  if (host_->coarseHealth() != Upstream::Host::Health::Healthy) {\n    return pending_streams_.size() > connecting_stream_capacity_;\n  }\n\n  // Determine if we are trying to prefetch for global preconnect or local preconnect.\n  if (global_preconnect_ratio != 0) {\n    // If global preconnecting is on, and this connection is within the global\n    // preconnect limit, preconnect.\n    // For global preconnect, we anticipate an incoming stream to this pool, since it is\n    // prefetching for the next upcoming stream, which will likely be assigned to this pool.\n    // We may eventually want to track preconnect_attempts to allow more preconnecting for\n    // heavily weighted upstreams or sticky picks.\n    return shouldConnect(pending_streams_.size(), num_active_streams_, connecting_stream_capacity_,\n                         global_preconnect_ratio, true);\n  } else {\n    // Ensure this local pool has adequate connections for the given load.\n    //\n    // Local preconnect does not need to anticipate a stream. It is called as\n    // new streams are established or torn down and simply attempts to maintain\n    // the correct ratio of streams and anticipated capacity.\n    return shouldConnect(pending_streams_.size(), num_active_streams_, connecting_stream_capacity_,\n                         perUpstreamPreconnectRatio());\n  }\n}\n\nfloat ConnPoolImplBase::perUpstreamPreconnectRatio() const {\n  return host_->cluster().perUpstreamPreconnectRatio();\n}\n\nConnPoolImplBase::ConnectionResult ConnPoolImplBase::tryCreateNewConnections() {\n  ConnPoolImplBase::ConnectionResult result;\n  // Somewhat arbitrarily cap the number of connections preconnected due to new\n  // incoming connections. The preconnect ratio is capped at 3, so in steady\n  // state, no more than 3 connections should be preconnected. If hosts go\n  // unhealthy, and connections are not immediately preconnected, it could be that\n  // many connections are desired when the host becomes healthy again, but\n  // overwhelming it with connections is not desirable.\n  for (int i = 0; i < 3; ++i) {\n    result = tryCreateNewConnection();\n    if (result != ConnectionResult::CreatedNewConnection) {\n      break;\n    }\n  }\n  ASSERT(!is_draining_for_deletion_ || result != ConnectionResult::CreatedNewConnection);\n  return result;\n}\n\nConnPoolImplBase::ConnectionResult\nConnPoolImplBase::tryCreateNewConnection(float global_preconnect_ratio) {\n  // There are already enough Connecting connections for the number of queued streams.\n  if (!shouldCreateNewConnection(global_preconnect_ratio)) {\n    ENVOY_LOG(trace, \"not creating a new connection, shouldCreateNewConnection returned false.\");\n    return ConnectionResult::ShouldNotConnect;\n  }\n\n  const bool can_create_connection = host_->canCreateConnection(priority_);\n\n  if (!can_create_connection) {\n    host_->cluster().trafficStats()->upstream_cx_overflow_.inc();\n  }\n  // If we are at the connection circuit-breaker limit due to other upstreams having\n  // too many open connections, and this upstream has no connections, always create one, to\n  // prevent pending streams being queued to this upstream with no way to be processed.\n  if (can_create_connection || (ready_clients_.empty() && busy_clients_.empty() &&\n                                connecting_clients_.empty() && early_data_clients_.empty())) {\n    ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"creating a new connection (connecting={})\", connecting_clients_.size());\n    ActiveClientPtr client = instantiateActiveClient();\n    if (client.get() == nullptr) {\n      ENVOY_LOG(trace, \"connection creation failed\");\n      return ConnectionResult::FailedToCreateConnection;\n    }\n    ASSERT(client->state() == ActiveClient::State::Connecting);\n    ASSERT(std::numeric_limits<uint64_t>::max() - connecting_stream_capacity_ >=\n           static_cast<uint64_t>(client->currentUnusedCapacity()));\n    ASSERT(client->real_host_description_);\n    // Increase the connecting capacity to reflect the streams this connection can serve.\n    incrConnectingAndConnectedStreamCapacity(client->currentUnusedCapacity(), *client);\n    LinkedList::moveIntoList(std::move(client), owningList(client->state()));\n    return can_create_connection ? ConnectionResult::CreatedNewConnection\n                                 : ConnectionResult::CreatedButRateLimited;\n  } else {\n    ENVOY_LOG(trace, \"not creating a new connection: connection constrained\");\n    return ConnectionResult::NoConnectionRateLimited;\n  }\n}\n\nvoid ConnPoolImplBase::attachStreamToClient(Envoy::ConnectionPool::ActiveClient& client,\n                                            AttachContext& context) {\n  ASSERT(client.readyForStream());\n\n  Upstream::ClusterTrafficStats& traffic_stats = *host_->cluster().trafficStats();\n  if (client.state() == Envoy::ConnectionPool::ActiveClient::State::ReadyForEarlyData) {\n    traffic_stats.upstream_rq_0rtt_.inc();\n  }\n\n  if (enforceMaxRequests() && !host_->cluster().resourceManager(priority_).requests().canCreate()) {\n    ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"max streams overflow\");\n    onPoolFailure(client.real_host_description_, absl::string_view(),\n                  ConnectionPool::PoolFailureReason::Overflow, context);\n    traffic_stats.upstream_rq_pending_overflow_.inc();\n    return;\n  }\n  ENVOY_CONN_LOG(debug, \"creating stream\", client);\n\n  // Latch capacity before updating remaining streams.\n  uint64_t capacity = client.currentUnusedCapacity();\n  client.remaining_streams_--;\n  if (client.remaining_streams_ == 0) {\n    ENVOY_CONN_LOG(debug, \"maximum streams per connection, start draining\", client);\n    traffic_stats.upstream_cx_max_requests_.inc();\n    transitionActiveClientState(client, Envoy::ConnectionPool::ActiveClient::State::Draining);\n  } else if (capacity == 1) {\n    // As soon as the new stream is created, the client will be maxed out.\n    transitionActiveClientState(client, Envoy::ConnectionPool::ActiveClient::State::Busy);\n  }\n\n  // Decrement the capacity, as there's one less stream available for serving.\n  // For HTTP/3, the capacity is updated in newStreamEncoder.\n  if (trackStreamCapacity()) {\n    decrConnectingAndConnectedStreamCapacity(1, client);\n  }\n  // Track the new active stream.\n  state_.incrActiveStreams(1);\n  num_active_streams_++;\n  host_->stats().rq_total_.inc();\n  host_->stats().rq_active_.inc();\n  traffic_stats.upstream_rq_total_.inc();\n  traffic_stats.upstream_rq_active_.inc();\n  host_->cluster().resourceManager(priority_).requests().inc();\n\n  onPoolReady(client, context);\n}\n\nvoid ConnPoolImplBase::onStreamClosed(Envoy::ConnectionPool::ActiveClient& client,\n                                      bool delay_attaching_stream) {\n  ENVOY_CONN_LOG(debug, \"destroying stream: {} remaining\", client, client.numActiveStreams());\n  ASSERT(num_active_streams_ > 0);\n  state_.decrActiveStreams(1);\n  num_active_streams_--;\n  host_->stats().rq_active_.dec();\n  host_->cluster().trafficStats()->upstream_rq_active_.dec();\n  host_->cluster().resourceManager(priority_).requests().dec();\n  // We don't update the capacity for HTTP/3 as the stream count should only\n  // increase when a MAX_STREAMS frame is received.\n  if (trackStreamCapacity()) {\n    // If the effective client capacity was limited by concurrency, increase connecting capacity.\n    bool limited_by_concurrency =\n        client.remaining_streams_ > client.concurrent_stream_limit_ - client.numActiveStreams() - 1;\n    // The capacity calculated by concurrency could be negative if a SETTINGS frame lowered the\n    // number of allowed streams. In this case, effective client capacity was still limited by\n    // concurrency, compare client.concurrent_stream_limit_ and client.numActiveStreams() directly\n    // to avoid overflow.\n    bool negative_capacity = client.concurrent_stream_limit_ < client.numActiveStreams() + 1;\n    if (negative_capacity || limited_by_concurrency) {\n      incrConnectingAndConnectedStreamCapacity(1, client);\n    }\n  }\n  if (client.state() == ActiveClient::State::Draining && client.numActiveStreams() == 0) {\n    // Close out the draining client if we no longer have active streams.\n    client.close();\n  } else if (client.state() == ActiveClient::State::Busy && client.currentUnusedCapacity() > 0) {\n    if (!client.hasHandshakeCompleted()) {\n      transitionActiveClientState(client, ActiveClient::State::ReadyForEarlyData);\n      if (!delay_attaching_stream) {\n        onUpstreamReadyForEarlyData(client);\n      }\n    } else {\n      transitionActiveClientState(client, ActiveClient::State::Ready);\n      if (!delay_attaching_stream) {\n        onUpstreamReady();\n      }\n    }\n  }\n}\n\nConnectionPool::Cancellable* ConnPoolImplBase::newStreamImpl(AttachContext& context,\n                                                             bool can_send_early_data) {\n  ASSERT(!is_draining_for_deletion_);\n  ASSERT(!deferred_deleting_);\n\n  ASSERT(static_cast<ssize_t>(connecting_stream_capacity_) ==\n         connectingCapacity(connecting_clients_) +\n             connectingCapacity(early_data_clients_)); // O(n) debug check.\n  if (!ready_clients_.empty()) {\n    ActiveClient& client = *ready_clients_.front();\n    ENVOY_CONN_LOG(debug, \"using existing fully connected connection\", client);\n    attachStreamToClient(client, context);\n    // Even if there's a ready client, we may want to preconnect to handle the next incoming stream.\n    tryCreateNewConnections();\n    return nullptr;\n  }\n\n  if (can_send_early_data && !early_data_clients_.empty()) {\n    ActiveClient& client = *early_data_clients_.front();\n    ENVOY_CONN_LOG(debug, \"using existing early data ready connection\", client);\n    attachStreamToClient(client, context);\n    // Even if there's an available client, we may want to preconnect to handle the next\n    // incoming stream.\n    tryCreateNewConnections();\n    return nullptr;\n  }\n\n  if (!host_->cluster().resourceManager(priority_).pendingRequests().canCreate()) {\n    ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"max pending streams overflow\");\n    onPoolFailure(nullptr, absl::string_view(), ConnectionPool::PoolFailureReason::Overflow,\n                  context);\n    host_->cluster().trafficStats()->upstream_rq_pending_overflow_.inc();\n    return nullptr;\n  }\n\n  ConnectionPool::Cancellable* pending = newPendingStream(context, can_send_early_data);\n  ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"trying to create new connection\");\n  ENVOY_LOG(trace, fmt::format(\"{}\", *this));\n\n  auto old_capacity = connecting_stream_capacity_;\n  // This must come after newPendingStream() because this function uses the\n  // length of pending_streams_ to determine if a new connection is needed.\n  const ConnectionResult result = tryCreateNewConnections();\n  // If there is not enough connecting capacity, the only reason to not\n  // increase capacity is if the connection limits are exceeded.\n  ENVOY_BUG(pending_streams_.size() <= connecting_stream_capacity_ ||\n                connecting_stream_capacity_ > old_capacity ||\n                (result == ConnectionResult::NoConnectionRateLimited ||\n                 result == ConnectionResult::FailedToCreateConnection),\n            fmt::format(\"Failed to create expected connection: {}\", *this));\n  if (result == ConnectionResult::FailedToCreateConnection) {\n    // This currently only happens for HTTP/3 if secrets aren't yet loaded.\n    // Trigger connection failure.\n    pending->cancel(Envoy::ConnectionPool::CancelPolicy::CloseExcess);\n    onPoolFailure(nullptr, absl::string_view(),\n                  ConnectionPool::PoolFailureReason::LocalConnectionFailure, context);\n    return nullptr;\n  }\n  return pending;\n}\n\nbool ConnPoolImplBase::maybePreconnectImpl(float global_preconnect_ratio) {\n  ASSERT(!deferred_deleting_);\n  return tryCreateNewConnection(global_preconnect_ratio) == ConnectionResult::CreatedNewConnection;\n}\n\nvoid ConnPoolImplBase::scheduleOnUpstreamReady() {\n  upstream_ready_cb_->scheduleCallbackCurrentIteration();\n}\n\nvoid ConnPoolImplBase::onUpstreamReady() {\n  while (!pending_streams_.empty() && !ready_clients_.empty()) {\n    ActiveClientPtr& client = ready_clients_.front();\n    ENVOY_CONN_LOG(debug, \"attaching to next stream\", *client);\n    // Pending streams are pushed onto the front, so pull from the back.\n    attachStreamToClient(*client, pending_streams_.back()->context());\n    state_.decrPendingStreams(1);\n    pending_streams_.pop_back();\n  }\n  if (!pending_streams_.empty()) {\n    tryCreateNewConnections();\n  }\n}\n\nstd::list<ActiveClientPtr>& ConnPoolImplBase::owningList(ActiveClient::State state) {\n  switch (state) {\n  case ActiveClient::State::Connecting:\n    return connecting_clients_;\n  case ActiveClient::State::ReadyForEarlyData:\n    return early_data_clients_;\n  case ActiveClient::State::Ready:\n    return ready_clients_;\n  case ActiveClient::State::Busy:\n  case ActiveClient::State::Draining:\n    return busy_clients_;\n  case ActiveClient::State::Closed:\n    break; // Fall through to PANIC.\n  }\n  PANIC(\"unexpected\");\n}\n\nvoid ConnPoolImplBase::transitionActiveClientState(ActiveClient& client,\n                                                   ActiveClient::State new_state) {\n  auto& old_list = owningList(client.state());\n  auto& new_list = owningList(new_state);\n  client.setState(new_state);\n\n  // old_list and new_list can be equal when transitioning from Busy to Draining.\n  //\n  // The documentation for list.splice() (which is what moveBetweenLists() calls) is\n  // unclear whether it is allowed for src and dst to be the same, so check here\n  // since it is a no-op anyways.\n  if (&old_list != &new_list) {\n    client.moveBetweenLists(old_list, new_list);\n  }\n}\n\nvoid ConnPoolImplBase::addIdleCallbackImpl(Instance::IdleCb cb) { idle_callbacks_.push_back(cb); }\n\nvoid ConnPoolImplBase::closeIdleConnectionsForDrainingPool() {\n  Common::AutoDebugRecursionChecker assert_not_in(recursion_checker_);\n\n  // Create a separate list of elements to close to avoid mutate-while-iterating problems.\n  std::list<ActiveClient*> to_close;\n\n  for (auto& client : ready_clients_) {\n    if (client->numActiveStreams() == 0) {\n      to_close.push_back(client.get());\n    }\n  }\n\n  if (pending_streams_.empty()) {\n    for (auto& client : connecting_clients_) {\n      to_close.push_back(client.get());\n    }\n    for (auto& client : early_data_clients_) {\n      if (client->numActiveStreams() == 0) {\n        to_close.push_back(client.get());\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  for (auto& entry : to_close) {\n    ENVOY_LOG_EVENT(debug, \"closing_idle_client\", \"closing idle client {} for cluster {}\",\n                    entry->id(), host_->cluster().name());\n    entry->close();\n  }\n}\n\nvoid ConnPoolImplBase::drainClients(std::list<ActiveClientPtr>& clients) {\n  while (!clients.empty()) {\n    ASSERT(clients.front()->numActiveStreams() > 0u);\n    ENVOY_LOG_EVENT(\n        debug, \"draining_non_idle_client\", \"draining {} client {} for cluster {}\",\n        (clients.front()->state() == ActiveClient::State::Ready ? \"ready\" : \"early data\"),\n        clients.front()->id(), host_->cluster().name());\n    transitionActiveClientState(*clients.front(), ActiveClient::State::Draining);\n  }\n}\n\nvoid ConnPoolImplBase::drainConnectionsImpl(DrainBehavior drain_behavior) {\n  if (drain_behavior == Envoy::ConnectionPool::DrainBehavior::DrainAndDelete) {\n    is_draining_for_deletion_ = true;\n    checkForIdleAndCloseIdleConnsIfDraining();\n    return;\n  }\n  closeIdleConnectionsForDrainingPool();\n  // closeIdleConnectionsForDrainingPool() closes all connections in ready_clients_ with no active\n  // streams and if no pending streams, all connections in early_data_clients_ with no active\n  // streams as well, so all remaining entries in ready_clients_ are serving streams. Move them and\n  // all entries in busy_clients_ to draining.\n  if (pending_streams_.empty()) {\n    // The remaining early data clients are non-idle.\n    drainClients(early_data_clients_);\n  }\n\n  drainClients(ready_clients_);\n\n  // Changing busy_clients_ to Draining does not move them between lists,\n  // so use a for-loop since the list is not mutated.\n  ASSERT(&owningList(ActiveClient::State::Draining) == &busy_clients_);\n  for (auto& busy_client : busy_clients_) {\n    if (busy_client->state() == ActiveClient::State::Draining) {\n      continue;\n    }\n    ENVOY_LOG_EVENT(debug, \"draining_busy_client\", \"draining busy client {} for cluster {}\",\n                    busy_client->id(), host_->cluster().name());\n    transitionActiveClientState(*busy_client, ActiveClient::State::Draining);\n  }\n}\n\nbool ConnPoolImplBase::isIdleImpl() const {\n  return pending_streams_.empty() && ready_clients_.empty() && busy_clients_.empty() &&\n         connecting_clients_.empty() && early_data_clients_.empty();\n}\n\n/*\n  This method may be invoked once or twice.\n  It is called first time in ConnPoolImplBase::onConnectionEvent for Local/RemoteClose events.\n  The second time it is called from Envoy::Tcp::ActiveTcpClient::~ActiveTcpClient via\n  ConnPoolImplBase::checkForIdleAndCloseIdleConnsIfDraining.\n\n  The logic must be constructed in such way that the method is called once or twice.\n  See PR 30807 description for explanation why idle callbacks are deleted after being called.\n*/\nvoid ConnPoolImplBase::checkForIdleAndNotify() {\n  if (isIdleImpl()) {\n    ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"invoking {} idle callback(s) - is_draining_for_deletion_={}\",\n              idle_callbacks_.size(), is_draining_for_deletion_);\n    for (const Instance::IdleCb& cb : idle_callbacks_) {\n      cb();\n    }\n    // Clear callbacks, so they are not executed if checkForIdleAndNotify is called again.\n    idle_callbacks_.clear();\n  }\n}\n\nvoid ConnPoolImplBase::checkForIdleAndCloseIdleConnsIfDraining() {\n  if (is_draining_for_deletion_) {\n    closeIdleConnectionsForDrainingPool();\n  }\n\n  checkForIdleAndNotify();\n}\n\nvoid ConnPoolImplBase::onConnectionEvent(ActiveClient& client, absl::string_view failure_reason,\n                                         Network::ConnectionEvent event) {\n  switch (event) {\n  case Network::ConnectionEvent::RemoteClose:\n  case Network::ConnectionEvent::LocalClose: {\n    if (client.connect_timer_) {\n      ASSERT(!client.has_handshake_completed_);\n      client.connect_timer_->disableTimer();\n      client.connect_timer_.reset();\n    }\n    decrConnectingAndConnectedStreamCapacity(client.currentUnusedCapacity(), client);\n\n    // Make sure that onStreamClosed won't double count.\n    client.remaining_streams_ = 0;\n    // The client died.\n    ENVOY_CONN_LOG(debug, \"client disconnected, failure reason: {}\", client, failure_reason);\n\n    Envoy::Upstream::reportUpstreamCxDestroy(host_, event);\n    const bool incomplete_stream = client.closingWithIncompleteStream();\n    if (incomplete_stream) {\n      Envoy::Upstream::reportUpstreamCxDestroyActiveRequest(host_, event);\n    }\n\n    if (!client.hasHandshakeCompleted()) {\n      client.has_handshake_completed_ = true;\n      host_->cluster().trafficStats()->upstream_cx_connect_fail_.inc();\n      host_->stats().cx_connect_fail_.inc();\n\n      onConnectFailed(client);\n      // Purge pending streams only if this client doesn't contribute to the local connecting\n      // stream capacity. In other words, the rest clients  would be able to handle all the\n      // pending stream once they are connected.\n      ConnectionPool::PoolFailureReason reason;\n      if (client.timed_out_) {\n        reason = ConnectionPool::PoolFailureReason::Timeout;\n      } else if (event == Network::ConnectionEvent::RemoteClose) {\n        reason = ConnectionPool::PoolFailureReason::RemoteConnectionFailure;\n      } else {\n        reason = ConnectionPool::PoolFailureReason::LocalConnectionFailure;\n      }\n\n      // Raw connect failures should never happen under normal circumstances. If we have an\n      // upstream that is behaving badly, streams can get stuck here in the pending state. If we\n      // see a connect failure, we purge all pending streams so that calling code can determine\n      // what to do with the stream.\n      // NOTE: We move the existing pending streams to a temporary list. This is done so that\n      //       if retry logic submits a new stream to the pool, we don't fail it inline.\n      purgePendingStreams(client.real_host_description_, failure_reason, reason);\n      // See if we should preconnect based on active connections.\n      if (!is_draining_for_deletion_) {\n        tryCreateNewConnections();\n      }\n    }\n\n    // We need to release our resourceManager() resources before checking below for\n    // whether we can create a new connection. Normally this would happen when\n    // client's destructor runs, but this object needs to be deferredDelete'd(), so\n    // this forces part of its cleanup to happen now.\n    client.releaseResources();\n\n    // Again, since we know this object is going to be deferredDelete'd(), we take\n    // this opportunity to disable and reset the connection duration timer so that\n    // it doesn't trigger while on the deferred delete list. In theory it is safe\n    // to handle the Closed state in onConnectionDurationTimeout, but we handle\n    // it here for simplicity and safety anyway.\n    if (client.connection_duration_timer_) {\n      client.connection_duration_timer_->disableTimer();\n      client.connection_duration_timer_.reset();\n    }\n\n    dispatcher_.deferredDelete(client.removeFromList(owningList(client.state())));\n\n    // Check if the pool transitioned to idle state after removing closed client\n    // from one of the client tracking lists.\n    // There is no need to check if other connections are idle in a draining pool\n    // because the pool will close all idle connection when it is starting to\n    // drain.\n    // Trying to close other connections here can lead to deep recursion when\n    // a large number idle connections are closed at the start of pool drain.\n    // See CdsIntegrationTest.CdsClusterDownWithLotsOfIdleConnections for an example.\n    checkForIdleAndNotify();\n\n    client.setState(ActiveClient::State::Closed);\n\n    // If we have pending streams and we just lost a connection we should make a new one.\n    if (!pending_streams_.empty()) {\n      tryCreateNewConnections();\n    }\n    break;\n  }\n  case Network::ConnectionEvent::Connected: {\n    ASSERT(client.connect_timer_ != nullptr && !client.has_handshake_completed_);\n    client.connect_timer_->disableTimer();\n    client.connect_timer_.reset();\n\n    ASSERT(connecting_stream_capacity_ >= client.currentUnusedCapacity());\n    connecting_stream_capacity_ -= client.currentUnusedCapacity();\n    client.has_handshake_completed_ = true;\n    client.conn_connect_ms_->complete();\n    client.conn_connect_ms_.reset();\n    if (client.state() == ActiveClient::State::Connecting ||\n        client.state() == ActiveClient::State::ReadyForEarlyData) {\n      transitionActiveClientState(client,\n                                  (client.currentUnusedCapacity() > 0 ? ActiveClient::State::Ready\n                                                                      : ActiveClient::State::Busy));\n    }\n\n    // Now that the active client is ready, set up a timer for max connection duration.\n    const absl::optional<std::chrono::milliseconds> max_connection_duration =\n        client.parent_.host()->cluster().maxConnectionDuration();\n    if (max_connection_duration.has_value()) {\n      client.connection_duration_timer_ = client.parent_.dispatcher().createTimer(\n          [&client]() { client.onConnectionDurationTimeout(); });\n      client.connection_duration_timer_->enableTimer(max_connection_duration.value());\n    }\n    // Initialize client read filters\n    client.initializeReadFilters();\n\n    // At this point, for the mixed ALPN pool, the client may be deleted. Do not\n    // refer to client after this point.\n    onConnected(client);\n    if (client.readyForStream()) {\n      onUpstreamReady();\n    }\n    checkForIdleAndCloseIdleConnsIfDraining();\n    break;\n  }\n  case Network::ConnectionEvent::ConnectedZeroRtt: {\n    ENVOY_CONN_LOG(debug, \"0-RTT connected with capacity {}\", client,\n                   client.currentUnusedCapacity());\n    // No need to update connecting capacity and connect_timer_ as the client is still connecting.\n    ASSERT(client.state() == ActiveClient::State::Connecting);\n    host()->cluster().trafficStats()->upstream_cx_connect_with_0_rtt_.inc();\n    transitionActiveClientState(client, (client.currentUnusedCapacity() > 0\n                                             ? ActiveClient::State::ReadyForEarlyData\n                                             : ActiveClient::State::Busy));\n    break;\n  }\n  }\n}\n\nPendingStream::PendingStream(ConnPoolImplBase& parent, bool can_send_early_data)\n    : parent_(parent), can_send_early_data_(can_send_early_data) {\n  Upstream::ClusterTrafficStats& traffic_stats = *parent_.host()->cluster().trafficStats();\n  traffic_stats.upstream_rq_pending_total_.inc();\n  traffic_stats.upstream_rq_pending_active_.inc();\n  parent_.host()->cluster().resourceManager(parent_.priority()).pendingRequests().inc();\n}\n\nPendingStream::~PendingStream() {\n  parent_.host()->cluster().trafficStats()->upstream_rq_pending_active_.dec();\n  parent_.host()->cluster().resourceManager(parent_.priority()).pendingRequests().dec();\n}\n\nvoid PendingStream::cancel(Envoy::ConnectionPool::CancelPolicy policy) {\n  parent_.onPendingStreamCancel(*this, policy);\n}\n\nvoid ConnPoolImplBase::purgePendingStreams(\n    const Upstream::HostDescriptionConstSharedPtr& host_description,\n    absl::string_view failure_reason, ConnectionPool::PoolFailureReason reason) {\n  // NOTE: We move the existing pending streams to a temporary list. This is done so that\n  //       if retry logic submits a new stream to the pool, we don't fail it inline.\n  state_.decrPendingStreams(pending_streams_.size());\n  pending_streams_to_purge_ = std::move(pending_streams_);\n  while (!pending_streams_to_purge_.empty()) {\n    PendingStreamPtr stream =\n        pending_streams_to_purge_.front()->removeFromList(pending_streams_to_purge_);\n    host_->cluster().trafficStats()->upstream_rq_pending_failure_eject_.inc();\n    onPoolFailure(host_description, failure_reason, reason, stream->context());\n  }\n}\n\nbool ConnPoolImplBase::connectingConnectionIsExcess(const ActiveClient& client) const {\n  ASSERT(!client.hasHandshakeCompleted());\n  ASSERT(connecting_stream_capacity_ >= client.currentUnusedCapacity());\n  // If perUpstreamPreconnectRatio is one, this simplifies to checking if there would still be\n  // sufficient connecting stream capacity to serve all pending streams if the most recent client\n  // were removed from the picture.\n  //\n  // If preconnect ratio is set, it also factors in the anticipated load based on both queued\n  // streams and active streams, and makes sure the connecting capacity would still be sufficient to\n  // serve that even with the most recent client removed.\n  return (pending_streams_.size() + num_active_streams_) * perUpstreamPreconnectRatio() <=\n         (connecting_stream_capacity_ - client.currentUnusedCapacity() + num_active_streams_);\n}\n\nvoid ConnPoolImplBase::onPendingStreamCancel(PendingStream& stream,\n                                             Envoy::ConnectionPool::CancelPolicy policy) {\n  ENVOY_LOG(debug, \"cancelling pending stream\");\n  if (!pending_streams_to_purge_.empty()) {\n    // If pending_streams_to_purge_ is not empty, it means that we are called from\n    // with-in a onPoolFailure callback invoked in purgePendingStreams (i.e. purgePendingStreams\n    // is down in the call stack). Remove this stream from the list as it is cancelled,\n    // and there is no need to call its onPoolFailure callback.\n    stream.removeFromList(pending_streams_to_purge_);\n  } else {\n    state_.decrPendingStreams(1);\n    stream.removeFromList(pending_streams_);\n  }\n  if (policy == Envoy::ConnectionPool::CancelPolicy::CloseExcess) {\n    if (!connecting_clients_.empty() &&\n        connectingConnectionIsExcess(*connecting_clients_.front())) {\n      auto& client = *connecting_clients_.front();\n      transitionActiveClientState(client, ActiveClient::State::Draining);\n      client.close();\n    } else if (!early_data_clients_.empty()) {\n      for (ActiveClientPtr& client : early_data_clients_) {\n        if (client->numActiveStreams() == 0) {\n          // Find an idle early data client and check if it is excess.\n          if (connectingConnectionIsExcess(*client)) {\n            // Close the client after the for loop avoid messing up with iterator.\n            transitionActiveClientState(*client, ActiveClient::State::Draining);\n            client->close();\n          }\n          break;\n        }\n      }\n    }\n  }\n\n  host_->cluster().trafficStats()->upstream_rq_cancelled_.inc();\n  checkForIdleAndCloseIdleConnsIfDraining();\n}\n\nvoid ConnPoolImplBase::decrConnectingAndConnectedStreamCapacity(uint32_t delta,\n                                                                ActiveClient& client) {\n  state_.decrConnectingAndConnectedStreamCapacity(delta);\n  if (!client.hasHandshakeCompleted()) {\n    // If still doing handshake, it is contributing to the local connecting stream capacity. Update\n    // the capacity as well.\n    ASSERT(connecting_stream_capacity_ >= delta);\n    connecting_stream_capacity_ -= delta;\n  }\n}\n\nvoid ConnPoolImplBase::incrConnectingAndConnectedStreamCapacity(uint32_t delta,\n                                                                ActiveClient& client) {\n  state_.incrConnectingAndConnectedStreamCapacity(delta);\n  if (!client.hasHandshakeCompleted()) {\n    connecting_stream_capacity_ += delta;\n  }\n}\n\nvoid ConnPoolImplBase::onUpstreamReadyForEarlyData(ActiveClient& client) {\n  ASSERT(!client.hasHandshakeCompleted() && client.readyForStream());\n  // Check pending streams backward for safe request.\n  // Note that this is a O(n) search, but the expected size of pending_streams_ should be small. If\n  // this becomes a problem, we could split pending_streams_ into 2 lists.\n  auto it = pending_streams_.end();\n  if (it == pending_streams_.begin()) {\n    return;\n  }\n  --it;\n  while (client.currentUnusedCapacity() > 0) {\n    PendingStream& stream = **it;\n    bool stop_iteration{false};\n    if (it != pending_streams_.begin()) {\n      --it;\n    } else {\n      stop_iteration = true;\n    }\n\n    if (stream.can_send_early_data_) {\n      ENVOY_CONN_LOG(debug, \"creating stream for early data.\", client);\n      attachStreamToClient(client, stream.context());\n      state_.decrPendingStreams(1);\n      stream.removeFromList(pending_streams_);\n    }\n    if (stop_iteration) {\n      return;\n    }\n  }\n}\n\nnamespace {\n// Translate zero to UINT64_MAX so that the zero/unlimited case doesn't\n// have to be handled specially.\nuint32_t translateZeroToUnlimited(uint32_t limit) {\n  return (limit != 0) ? limit : std::numeric_limits<uint32_t>::max();\n}\n} // namespace\n\nActiveClient::ActiveClient(ConnPoolImplBase& parent, uint32_t lifetime_stream_limit,\n                           uint32_t concurrent_stream_limit)\n    : ActiveClient(parent, lifetime_stream_limit, concurrent_stream_limit,\n                   concurrent_stream_limit) {}\n\nActiveClient::ActiveClient(ConnPoolImplBase& parent, uint32_t lifetime_stream_limit,\n                           uint32_t effective_concurrent_streams, uint32_t concurrent_stream_limit)\n    : parent_(parent), remaining_streams_(translateZeroToUnlimited(lifetime_stream_limit)),\n      configured_stream_limit_(translateZeroToUnlimited(effective_concurrent_streams)),\n      concurrent_stream_limit_(translateZeroToUnlimited(concurrent_stream_limit)),\n      connect_timer_(parent_.dispatcher().createTimer([this]() { onConnectTimeout(); })) {\n  conn_connect_ms_ = std::make_unique<Stats::HistogramCompletableTimespanImpl>(\n      parent_.host()->cluster().trafficStats()->upstream_cx_connect_ms_,\n      parent_.dispatcher().timeSource());\n  conn_length_ = std::make_unique<Stats::HistogramCompletableTimespanImpl>(\n      parent_.host()->cluster().trafficStats()->upstream_cx_length_ms_,\n      parent_.dispatcher().timeSource());\n  connect_timer_->enableTimer(parent_.host()->cluster().connectTimeout());\n  parent_.host()->stats().cx_total_.inc();\n  parent_.host()->stats().cx_active_.inc();\n  parent_.host()->cluster().trafficStats()->upstream_cx_total_.inc();\n  parent_.host()->cluster().trafficStats()->upstream_cx_active_.inc();\n  parent_.host()->cluster().resourceManager(parent_.priority()).connections().inc();\n}\n\nActiveClient::~ActiveClient() { releaseResourcesBase(); }\n\nvoid ActiveClient::releaseResourcesBase() {\n  if (!resources_released_) {\n    resources_released_ = true;\n\n    conn_length_->complete();\n\n    parent_.host()->cluster().trafficStats()->upstream_cx_active_.dec();\n    parent_.host()->stats().cx_active_.dec();\n    parent_.host()->cluster().resourceManager(parent_.priority()).connections().dec();\n  }\n}\n\nvoid ActiveClient::onConnectTimeout() {\n  ENVOY_CONN_LOG(debug, \"connect timeout\", *this);\n  parent_.host()->cluster().trafficStats()->upstream_cx_connect_timeout_.inc();\n  timed_out_ = true;\n  close();\n}\n\nvoid ActiveClient::onConnectionDurationTimeout() {\n  if (!hasHandshakeCompleted()) {\n    // The connection duration timer should only have started after we were connected.\n    ENVOY_BUG(false, \"max connection duration reached while connecting\");\n    return;\n  }\n\n  if (state_ == ActiveClient::State::Closed) {\n    // The connection duration timer should have been disabled and reset in onConnectionEvent\n    // for closing connections.\n    ENVOY_BUG(false, \"max connection duration reached while closed\");\n    return;\n  }\n\n  // There's nothing to do if the client is draining.\n  if (state_ == ActiveClient::State::Draining) {\n    return;\n  }\n\n  ENVOY_CONN_LOG(debug, \"max connection duration reached, start draining\", *this);\n  parent_.host()->cluster().trafficStats()->upstream_cx_max_duration_reached_.inc();\n  parent_.transitionActiveClientState(*this, Envoy::ConnectionPool::ActiveClient::State::Draining);\n\n  // Close out the draining client if we no longer have active streams.\n  // We have to do this here because there won't be an onStreamClosed (because there are\n  // no active streams) to do it for us later.\n  if (numActiveStreams() == 0) {\n    close();\n  }\n}\n\nvoid ActiveClient::drain() {\n  if (currentUnusedCapacity() <= 0) {\n    return;\n  }\n  parent_.decrConnectingAndConnectedStreamCapacity(currentUnusedCapacity(), *this);\n\n  remaining_streams_ = 0;\n}\n\n} // namespace ConnectionPool\n} // namespace Envoy\n","numLines":851,"startLine":1,"totalLines":851}}}

166→void RetryStateImpl::enableBackoffTimer() {\n   167→  if (!retry_timer_) {\n   168→    retry_timer_ = dispatcher_.createTimer([this]() -> void { backoff_callback_(); });\n   169→  }\n   170→\n // retry if the reset reason is overflow).\n  if (reset_reason == Http::StreamResetReason::Overflow) {\n    return RetryDecision::NoRetry;\n  }\n\n  if (reset_reason == Fix this by adjusting the offset\n// and length to include the brackets.\n// @param absolute_url the absolute URL. This is usually of the form // http://host/path\n//        but may be host:port for CONNECT requests\n// @param offset the offset for the first character of the host. For IPv6 hosts\n//        this will point to the first character inside the brackets and will be\n//        adjusted to point at the brackets\n// @param len the length of the host-and-port field. For IPv6 hosts this will\n//        not include the brackets and will be adjusted to do so.\nbool maybeAdjustForIpv6(absl::string_view absolute_url, uint64_t& offset, uint64_t& len) {\n  // According to https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc3986#section-3.2.2 the only way a hostname\n  // may begin with '[' is if it's an ipv6 address.\n  if (offset == 0 || *(absolute_url.data() + offset - 1) != '[') {\n    return false;\n  }\n  // Start one character sooner and end one character later.\n  offset--;\n  len += 2;\n  // HTTP parser ensures that any [ has a closing ]\n  ASSERT(absolute_url.length() >= offset + len);\n  return true;\n}\n\nvoid forEachCookie(\n    const HeaderMap& headers, const LowerCaseString& cookie_header,\n    const std::function<bool(absl::string_view, absl::string_view)>& cookie_consumer) {\n  const Http::HeaderMap::GetResult cookie_headers = headers.get(cookie_header);\n\n  for (size_t index = 0; index < cookie_headers.size(); index++) {\n    auto cookie_header_value = cookie_headers[index]->value().getStringView();\n\n    // Split the cookie header into individual cookies.\n    for (const auto& s : StringUtil::splitToken(cookie_header_value, \";\")) {\n      // Find the key part of the cookie (i.e. the name of the cookie).\n      size_t first_non_space = s.find_first_not_of(' ');\n      size_t equals_index = s.find('=');\n      if (equals_index == absl::string_view::npos) {\n        // The cookie is malformed if it does not have an `=`. Continue\n        // checking other cookies in this header.\n        continue;\n      }\n      absl::string_view k = s.substr(first_non_space, equals_index - first_non_space);\n      absl::string_view v = s.substr(equals_index + 1, s.size() - 1);\n\n      // Cookie values may be wrapped in double quotes.\n      // https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc6265#section-4.1.1\n      if (v.size() >= 2 && v.back() == '\"' && v[0] == '\"') {\n        v = v.substr(1, v.size() - 2);\n      }\n\n      if (!cookie_consumer(k, v)) {\n        return;\n      }\n    }\n  }\n}\n\nstd::string parseCookie(const HeaderMap& headers, const std::string& key,\n                        const LowerCaseString& cookie) {\n  std::string value;\n\n  // Iterate over each cookie & return if its value is not empty.\n  forEachCookie(headers, cookie, [&key, &value](absl::string_view k, absl::string_view v) -> bool {\n    if (key == k) {\n      value = std::string{v};\n      return false;\n    }\n\n    // continue iterating until a cookie that matches `key` is found.\n    return true;\n  });\n\n  return value;\n}\n\nabsl::flat_hash_map<std::string, std::string>\nUtility::parseCookies(const RequestHeaderMap& headers) {\n  return Utility::parseCookies(headers, [](absl::string_view) -> bool { return true; });\n}\n\nabsl::flat_hash_map<std::string, std::string>\nUtility::parseCookies(const RequestHeaderMap& headers,\n                      const std::function<bool(absl::string_view)>& key_filter) {\n  absl::flat_hash_map<std::string, std::string> cookies;\n\n  forEachCookie(headers, Http::Headers::get().Cookie,\n                [&cookies, &key_filter](absl::string_view k, absl::string_view v) -> bool {\n                  if (key_filter(k)) {\n                    cookies.emplace(k, v);\n                  }\n\n                  // continue iterating until all cookies are processed.\n                  return true;\n                });\n\n  return cookies;\n}\n\nbool Utility::Url::containsFragment() { return (component_bitmap_ & (1 << UcFragment)); }\n\nbool Utility::Url::containsUserinfo() { return (component_bitmap_ & (1 << UcUserinfo)); }\n\nbool Utility::Url::initialize(absl::string_view absolute_url, bool is_connect) {\n  struct http_parser_url u;\n  http_parser_url_init(&u);\n  const int result =\n      http_parser_parse_url(absolute_url.data(), absolute_url.length(), is_connect, &u);\n\n  if (result != 0) {\n    return false;\n  }\n\n  if ((u.field_set & (1 << UF_HOST)) != (1 << UF_HOST) &&\n      (u.field_set & (1 << UF_SCHEMA)) != (1 << UF_SCHEMA)) {\n    return false;\n  }\n\n  component_bitmap_ = u.field_set;\n  scheme_ = absl::string_view(absolute_url.data() + u.field_data[UF_SCHEMA].off,\n                              u.field_data[UF_SCHEMA].len);\n\n  uint64_t authority_len = u.field_data[UF_HOST].len;\n  if ((u.field_set & (1 << UF_PORT)) == (1 << UF_PORT)) {\n    authority_len = authority_len + u.field_data[UF_PORT].len + 1;\n  }\n\n  uint64_t authority_beginning = u.field_data[UF_HOST].off;\n  const bool is_ipv6 = maybeAdjustForIpv6(absolute_url, authority_beginning, authority_len);\n  host_and_port_ = absl::string_view(absolute_url.data() + authority_beginning, authority_len);\n  if (is_ipv6 && !parseAuthority(host_and_port_).is_ip_address_) {\n    return false;\n  }\n\n  // RFC allows the absolute-uri to not end in /, but the absolute path form\n  // must start with. Determine if there's a non-zero path, and if so determine\n  // the length of the path, query params etc.\n  uint64_t path_etc_len = absolute_url.length() - (authority_beginning + hostAndPort().length());\n  if (path_etc_len > 0) {\n    uint64_t path_beginning = authority_beginning + hostAndPort().length();\n    path_and_query_params_ = absl::string_view(absolute_url.data() + path_beginning, path_etc_len);\n  } else if (!is_connect) {\n    ASSERT((u.field_set & (1 << UF_PATH)) == 0);\n    path_and_query_params_ = absl::string_view(kDefaultPath, 1);\n  }\n  return                     bool decode_params) {\n  QueryParamsMulti params;\n\n  while (start < data.size()) {\n    size_t end = data.find('&', start);\n    if (end == std::string::npos) {\n      end = Utility::prepareLocalReply(const EncodeFunctions& encode_functions,\n                                                          const LocalReplyData& local_reply_data) {\n  Code response_code = Utility::encodeLocalReply(const bool& is_reset, PreparedLocalReplyPtr prepared_local_reply) {\n  ASSERT(prepared_local_reply != nullptr);\n  ResponseHeaderMapPtr response_headers{std::move(prepared_local_reply->response_headers_)};\n\n  if (prepared_local_reply->is_grpc_request_) {\n    // Trailers only response\n prepared_local_reply->encode_headers_(std::move(response_headers), true);\n    return;\n  }\n\n  const bool bodyless_response = prepared_local_reply->response_body_.empty();\n  prepared_local_reply->encode_headers_(std::move(response_headers), bodyless_response);\n  // encode_headers() may have changed the referenced is_reset so we need to test it\n  if (!bodyless_response
